session_01ÔøΩdefaultSessionÔøΩ  ÔøΩ` ÔøΩÔøΩÔøΩÔøΩÔøΩÔøΩ This diagnosticSession is used to enable timed diagnostic service functionality (e.g., I/O control). The diagnostic functionality in this session shall also include all supported diagnostic functionality supported in the defaultSession.ÔøΩ
